# Welcome | Bloom Solana

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FOPccEIBCShPoLnOD0wzd%252Fbloom_banner_2_final.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff8aaf60-35ea-447c-be3d-897deee17615&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0297aa1&sv=2)

Bloom is your all-in-one trading solution, built for speed, simplicity, and seamless performance, perfect whether you're just starting out or already a seasoned trader.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/#supported-blockchains)

Supported Blockchains:

**🟪 Solana**

**⬜️ Ethereum**

**🟨 BSC**

**🟦 Base**

**🟩 HyperEVM**

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/#why-choose-bloom)

Why Choose Bloom?

*   **Insanely Fast Fills**: Trade faster than ever with our optimized and fully rebuilt infrastructure.
    
*   **Hybrid Trading**: Combine advanced web-based extension settings and powerful Telegram tools for unmatched flexibility.
    
*   **Trade Anywhere, Anytime**: Seamlessly switch from desktop to mobile trading through our user-friendly Telegram bot.
    

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/#core-features)

Core Features:

*   **Spot Buy & Sell:** Instant trading made easy.
    
*   **Sniper:** Quickly catch new token opportunities.
    
*   **Copy-Trading:** Effortlessly copy successful traders in real-time.
    
*   **AFK Mode:** Automate your trading even when you're away.
    
*   **Chrome Extension:** Supercharge your trading terminal with advanced tools.
    
*   **Multiple Limit Orders:** Execute your strategies with precision.
    
*   **In-Bot Bridge:** Conveniently bridge tokens between blockchains within the bot.
    
*   **Advanced Settings:** Fully customize your trading experience to your style.
    

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/#supercharged-extension)

Supercharged Extension

Our Chrome Extension boosts your trading terminal with:

*   Faster trades
    
*   Rich customization
    
*   Easy wallet integration
    
*   Enhanced notifications
    

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/#rewards-and-benefits)

Rewards & Benefits

Enjoy fee discounts and an attractive referral program, increasing your earnings while trading.

[NextFirst Steps](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/first-steps)

# First Steps | Bloom Solana

It’s essential to manage your private key carefully. Please ensure you store it securely, as deleting the Telegram message shown below will make it permanently irretrievable for security reasons.

Once you’ve safely stored your private key, we strongly recommend deleting the Telegram message.

Follow the steps below to securely set up your account and get ready for trading.

* * *

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FPRrpAcHIKXZJrA7mXg4k%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2630ff34-41b8-49b7-a8e9-94e6f853396f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b109305&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/first-steps#start-trading)

Start Trading


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After completing the initial steps outlined above, simply tap `🚀 Start Trading` to enjoy Bloom full potential.

# Deposit | Bloom Solana

To begin trading on Bloom, you need to deposit **SOL** into the wallet created when you first joined the platform. Follow these steps to ensure your wallet is ready for trading.

Only deposit **SOL** through the **Solana network** to avoid losing funds. Always double-check your wallet address before confirming any transfers.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FPvZOPvkMCgHJraShQWpu%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f53e54b-54fa-48fe-a25e-ed4420a641af&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d64f8dda&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/wallets-setup/deposit#locate-your-wallet-address)

**Locate Your Wallet Address**

When you first joined Bloom, a wallet was automatically generated for you, and you can find your wallet address by navigating to the `Wallets` section in the menu or by running the `/wallets` command.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F1pldrAEfraJt0FfjZaVm%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ab5dd05-406b-434c-ae48-1380507a7f6b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca1f7177&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/wallets-setup/deposit#wait-for-the-deposit-confirmation)

**Wait for the Deposit Confirmation**

Once the transfer is initiated, it may take a few moments for the SOL to appear in your Bloom wallet. Just refresh the page to check if the deposit has arrived.

[PreviousMulti-Wallet](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/wallets-setup/multi-wallet)
[NextUseful Links](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/useful-links)

# Multi-Wallet | Bloom Solana

With Bloom, you can easily manage multiple wallets all in one place. Whether you're handling various portfolios or diversifying your trades, multi-wallet support gives you the flexibility to stay organized and efficient.

You can:

*   **Create, import, and manage multiple wallets** effortlessly from your account.
    
*   **Track positions and performance** across all wallets.
    
*   **Set a default wallet** for easy transactions, while having the option to switch between others as needed.
    

Refer to the [dedicated guide](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets)
 for more in-depth guidance.

[PreviousWallets Setup](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/wallets-setup)
[NextDeposit](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/wallets-setup/deposit)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Fee | Bloom Solana

On the Fee page, select the preset fees you want to use. They’ll automatically apply to each relevant module.

* * *

*   Access `⚙️ Settings` easily from the home menu or by using the `/settings`command.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FbgaXiaSbfRxMqYqMtwyQ%252FSettings.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd552293-8385-48b6-8ebd-88f2d507cf41&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=adc14266&sv=2)

*   Tap `⛽️ Fee`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FzRR9biBmFM70itch71kn%252FFee.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D182f8563-8578-44ba-865b-80b21c5f2130&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a25a8594&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FwybOvSGFtSDkuQwK2B8Z%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252018.31.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07f2a00c-7670-4c05-b09c-34a5762c2df9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef3440c5&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Buy Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Sell Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired sell fee amount in SOL:

Example:

• For a sell fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Buy Tip

Set the Jito buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip amount in SOL:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Sell Tip

Set the Jito sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip amount in SOL:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Auto Tip

If enabled, it automatically selects the Jito-suggested tip, ranging from 0.015 to 0.15.

_Priority fees are set to a fixed amount since the tip is what matters for Jito Blocks._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Back

Return to the previous page.

Close

Close the current menu.

# Slippage | Bloom Solana

Slippage is the difference between the expected price of a trade and the actual price at which the trade is executed. It typically occurs during periods of high volatility or low liquidity. Generally, the higher it is, the faster your transaction is but the higher are the chances of getting your transaction sandwiched.

* * *

*   Access `⚙️ Settings` easily from the home menu or by using the `/settings`command.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FbgaXiaSbfRxMqYqMtwyQ%252FSettings.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd552293-8385-48b6-8ebd-88f2d507cf41&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=adc14266&sv=2)

*   Tap `🛍️ Slippage`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FdQBcwFiVV6CqESCEgR9K%252FSlippage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfaa033bc-5e09-4e02-9f54-9f952da53697&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d09db67&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F89dpLQaF176LTcmOHO6Q%252FScreenshot%25202025-07-09%2520alle%252014.49.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81500a41-0626-4b43-a7f6-87ed27db7556&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7331be9&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Buy Slip

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Sell Slip

Set the sell slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

# Locations | Bloom Solana

🇩🇪 DE[](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/locations#de)

[https://t.me/BloomSolana](https://t.me/BloomSolana_bot)
[\_bot](https://t.me/BloomSolana_bot)

🇺🇸 US[](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/locations#us)

[https://t.me/BloomSolanaUS1\_bot](https://t.me/BloomSolanaUS1_bot)

* * *

Why multiple locations?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/getting-started/locations#why-multiple-locations)

Before we explain why we support multiple locations, note that there’s no functional difference between using one bot or another.

We support multiple locations to provide backup options in case of downtime and to optimize proximity to various validators.

Performance remains consistent across all bots, but if one experiences a higher workload, switching to a less busy option can improve response times.

# Presets | Bloom Solana

Presets allow you to save your favorite settings in advance, streamlining task creation and accelerating any trading action. Quickly access and reuse your preferred parameters, and conveniently set up Auto Orders ahead of time to align precisely with your buy and sell strategies.

*   Access `⚙️ Settings` easily from the home menu or by using the `/settings`command.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FdPzb0DfC0quoXyUeZlS9%252FSettings.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddcad5ca8-485c-4633-a1e4-a825f68e78ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dbe0ba62&sv=2)

*   Tap `🔧 Presets`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FM0GadimCg9dTNOO9xJWv%252FPresets.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbde5fc62-86de-441f-973e-cefb25fd75c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eb5e34d1&sv=2)

# Buy Presets | Bloom Solana

Buy Presets let you define the default amounts displayed for buying.

* * *

*   Tap `🔧 Buy Presets` from the Presets menu.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F2kNGLHeJcyTs3tEmJcNF%252FBuy.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D837b5e71-1ba0-4dd6-afa2-5e726fe2a1a3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf0ae47a&sv=2)

# Spot Presets • Auto Orders | Bloom Solana

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

After creation, the task will automatically start post-buy. Make sure to delete it if you don't want it to run.

* * *

*   Tap `📈 Spot Presets` from the Presets menu.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FXWzlB9d8SvQ4y6F8D0OX%252FSpot.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50b59ab6-c63a-432d-bc8d-d6fb3cf3b1a2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0c56dc6&sv=2)

*   Tap `🆕 Create Limit Order`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIOnv8S50bInsqZrZbcI9%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.33.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a877771-6084-4509-9218-b2aecdbcd453&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc9df95f&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F5A4PJZ0vNGVtgXRZ7e1C%252FScreenshot%25202025-07-07%2520alle%252017.42.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df96d5118-54c1-4830-bfe9-96576541fd37&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c31a1e30&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. 🟢: When enabled, Bloom will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Profit/Loss %

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

Fixed Mcap

Set the target market cap at which you’d like Bloom to sell.

Mcap Variation

Set the market cap increase or decrease threshold at which you’d like Bloom to sell. Bloom will execute the sale only when the market cap change matches your specified value.

Sell at

This button adapts based on your selected selling method (Profit/Loss %, Fixed MCap, MCap Variation), allowing you to set your preferred value accordingly.

Enter your target value:

• Take Profit: e.g. 50%, 150%.

• Stop Loss: e.g. -20%, -50%.

Examples:

• Profit %: 100%: your holdings will be sold at 2x.

• Loss %: -50%: your holdings will be sold when the price drops by 50%.

Notes:

• Only one % value (TP or SL) per limit order.

Sell Amount

Set the target amount to sell as a percentage.

Please enter your desired sell amount:

Example:

• For a sell of 10%, enter 10

Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

High Impact (Expert only)

Enables trades that require higher price impact than usual. Use this if you’re buying large amounts of SOL in low-liquidity pools. ⚠️ **Expert users only:** using this when it’s not needed can route the sale through suboptimal pools or cause bad slippage.

Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fc3BThte0PlgtZal4UqJj%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252019.04.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1df5a62-a21c-414b-bb1f-d4800b8b224b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e02e17e&sv=2)

[PreviousSell Presets](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/settings/presets/sell-presets)
[NextSniper Presets](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/settings/presets/sniper-presets)

# Degen Mode | Bloom Solana

Degen Mode instantly buys a token as soon as its contract address is entered in Telegram, without asking for additional details. Once typed, it will attempt to purchase based on your settings, regardless of your balance.

*   When enabled, Degen Mode will attempt to **buy immediately as soon as the token address is entered**, even before the token menu appears. It will try to execute the purchase regardless of the wallet balance.
    
*   Once the token is sold, it won’t attempt to rebuy, even if auto-buy is enabled.
    

**🟢 ON –** Automatically buy a coin when the coin address is pasted. 🔴 **OFF –** Manually start buy when the coin address is pasted.

* * *

*   Access `⚙️ Settings` easily from the home menu or by using the `/settings`command.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FbgaXiaSbfRxMqYqMtwyQ%252FSettings.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd552293-8385-48b6-8ebd-88f2d507cf41&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=adc14266&sv=2)

*   Tap `Degen Mode`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FOgHSIlBWN01flKWPWx5y%252FDegen.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb762210-f491-4f40-8df8-ebfa424ef40c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1a2c1b00&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fi4k4bdUtQuQwzNhObkGK%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252015.14.35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57b2cb79-df52-4cb8-bf1a-e18b7838d740&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e42bac41&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Degen State

Turn auto buy On and Off.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Platforms

Select the platforms you want Degen Mode to use. Only contracts matching these active platforms will trigger a purchase, while non-matching ones will be skipped.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F256EsweqUEnD3GZ0PdTR%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252015.16.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D18e78e81-107f-4cb8-8142-e0fcab898a1f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ea6b54b&sv=2)

Degen Amount

Choose the preset SOL amount to buy.

Please enter your desired buy amount in SOL:

Example:

• For a buy of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Degen Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage amount in %:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Min MCap

Set the minimum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Please enter your desired market cap or enter -1 to disable:

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

Examples:

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Max MCap

Set the maximum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Please enter your desired market cap or enter -1 to disable:

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

Examples:

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Min Liq

Set the minimum SOL liquidity needed to buy.

Please enter your desired liquidity value

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

_Examples:_

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Max Liq

Set the maximum SOL liquidity needed to buy.

Please enter your desired liquidity value

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

_Examples:_

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

# Copy Presets | Bloom Solana

Copy Presets allow you to set the default configurations used when running a copy-trading task.

* * *

*   Tap `🤖 Copy Presets` from the Presets menu.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FgHtAXtwzIRfjPutKF2My%252FCopy.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca7c1d37-99cb-4b4b-a2ac-e548740a5728&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=304b0cc8&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FhwykagwLjeh4kgeBl2aX%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252018.54.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94442dd0-cd64-4e9d-8982-e106a77d1ddf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=55ef4f95&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Platforms

Choose the platform to activate the AFK task on. After selection, set up the task, and AFK Mode will be enabled on all chosen platforms.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FM1fw22S9ddXVntZkFOkI%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252018.46.04.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D53cb15d0-15ed-4918-a8a9-938cfd28d853&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3baefc12&sv=2)

Max Buy Count

Set the maximum number of coins the bot will purchase according to your current configuration.

Please enter your desired number of tokens to trade or enter -1 to disable:

First Interaction

🟢: If enabled, it will trigger trades only when the trader you’re copy-trading interacts with the token for the first time 🔴: If disabled, the bot will not consider whether the trader has previously interacted with the token or not.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Max Buy

Set the maximum amount you’re willing to buy, regardless of the amount purchased by the target wallet. _**Max Buy applies to each transaction.**_

Please enter your desired max buy amount in SOL or enter -1 to disable:

Buy Exact

Buy the same SOL amount as the target wallet.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy %

Buy a percentage of the amount the target wallet buys. _You can set it above 100% to purchase more than the target wallet (eg. 130% buys an additional 30% of the amount purchased by the target wallet)._

Buy Fixed

Buy a fixed SOL amount, regardless of the target wallet’s amount.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Min Trigger Buy

Set the minimum SOL amount purchased by the target wallet required for your transaction to be executed.

Please enter your desired min trigger buy amount in SOL or enter -1 to disable:

Max Trigger Buy

Set the maximum SOL amount purchased by the target wallet required for your transaction to be executed.

Please enter your desired max trigger buy amount in SOL or enter -1 to disable:

Min MCap

Set the minimum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Please enter your desired market cap or enter -1 to disable:

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

Examples:

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Max MCap

Set the maximum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Please enter your desired market cap or enter -1 to disable:

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

Examples:

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Min Token Age

• Set the minimum amount of time passed since the token was created. • For Pump.fun migrated coins, the time is calculated from the moment they bonded.

Please enter the token age or enter -1 to disable:

📝 Format examples:

• 1H = 1 hour

• 30M = 30 minutes

• 1D = 1 day

• 60 = 60 seconds

Supported units:

• H = hours

• M = minutes

• D = days

• Direct number = seconds

Max Token Age

• Set the maximum amount of time passed since the token was created. • For Pump.fun migrated coins, the time is calculated from the moment they bonded.

Please enter the token age or enter -1 to disable:

📝 Format examples:

• 1H = 1 hour

• 30M = 30 minutes

• 1D = 1 day

• 60 = 60 seconds

Supported units:

• H = hours

• M = minutes

• D = days

• Direct number = seconds

Follow Sell

Choose whether to sell when the target wallet sells.

_When enabled, the bot will mirror the selling percentage of the trader - for example, if they sell 50% of their position, the bot will also sell 50% of your position_

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Only Once

Buy the coin only once, even if the target wallet makes multiple purchases. _If you’re using multiple wallets, ensure it’s turned ON for each one._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Sell Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Buy Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Sell Slippage

Set the sell slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Buy Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Sell Tip

Set the target sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Auto Orders


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

After creation, the task will automatically start post-buy. Make sure to delete it if you don't want it to run.

*   Click `📈 Limit Orders`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fpbi7IXYpA3u0jPckFhMz%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.32.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8716f39-a533-43f2-ba7d-439eec3becc2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9bb8dc78&sv=2)

*   Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIOnv8S50bInsqZrZbcI9%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.33.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a877771-6084-4509-9218-b2aecdbcd453&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc9df95f&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FhQ79mOyLoPSAR38Nz6xl%252FScreenshot%25202025-07-07%2520alle%252017.42.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa8ae116-6045-4f0e-a236-aeba6e194bd5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea5825d1&sv=2)

# Limit Orders | Bloom Solana

Limit orders allow you to set a specific price at which you want to buy or sell a cryptocurrency. Unlike market orders that execute immediately at the current price, limit orders only trigger when the market reaches your desired price or market cap.

Additionally, you can customize your order with multiple parameters, ensuring your trade is tailored to your strategy.

[PreviousSell](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/sell)
[NextLimit Buy](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/limit-orders/limit-buy)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Pro Accounts | Bloom Solana

**PRO Accounts are mandatory**. If the selected wallet doesn’t have one, Bloom will automatically attempt to create it. You’ll only see a confirmation, or a failure notification, once the creation transaction is processed.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#introduction-to-pro-accounts-v2.0)

Introduction to Pro Accounts (v2.0)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Pro Accounts in version 2.0 are designed to optimize the broadcasting of your transactions across the best validators and node providers. This ensures that each buy or sell transaction you execute is handled efficiently and lands only once, avoiding duplication.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#usage-recommendations)

Usage Recommendations


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For typical activities such as running several copy tasks, placing orders, and performing spot trades—we generally recommend:

*   **1 to 3 Spot Pro Accounts**
    
*   **4 Task Pro Accounts**
    

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#types-of-pro-accounts)

Types of Pro Accounts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Spot Accounts**[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#spot-accounts)

Used for any spot buy and sell operations, including those executed through our extension.

**Tasks Accounts**[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#tasks-accounts)

Used for copy-trading, AFK mode, and various types of orders.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#determining-the-number-of-pro-accounts-needed)

Determining the Number of Pro Accounts Needed


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The required number of Pro Accounts primarily depends on how many tasks you trigger at the same time. For instance, if you have only one Pro Account and two copy tasks that need to execute transactions simultaneously, only one transaction will successfully land.

In short, the more tasks you plan to run simultaneously, the more Pro Accounts you'll need to create.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#cost)

Cost


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each Pro Account requires a maximum of **0.002 SOL** for its creation.

[PreviousWallets](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets)
[NextBuy](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/buy)

Last updated 13 days ago

---

# Active Orders | Bloom Solana

*   This menu provides an overview of all your current open orders for the selected coin. By clicking `🗑️ Delete Order`, you can cancel the corresponding order displayed on the left.

# Limit Sell | Bloom Solana

**Sell Fee:** The buy fee is taken from the default one in [settings](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/settings/fee)
.

**Orders expiration –** Expired orders are automatically deleted.

* * *

*   Start a regular [Sell](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/sell)
    task by entering the token address.
    
*   Tap `📈 Limit Orders`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fhv44MTzoFEXwBazT9lXv%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df70967a6-0428-4f8f-b9cb-658366f2572a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=782f88af&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fv60ISLuVkKrsXMbabxYl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf94eef1-918e-4a68-989e-655058099aec&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c335eb9&sv=2)

Action

Response

Set the order expiration time in hours (eg. 6).

Sell Amount

Choose the % to sell.

Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

High Impact (Expert only)

Allows selling with higher price impact than usual. Useful for large sell orders in low-liquidity pools.

⚠️ _**Expert users only:**_ _using this when it’s not needed can route the sale through suboptimal pools or cause bad slippage._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically buy the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. If enabled, the bot will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

• Choose to create the order based on market cap. • Enter the target market cap value.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Create Limit Order

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/limit-orders/limit-sell#take-profit)

Take Profit


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set multiple Take Profits, create separate orders with different market caps/prices and percentages aligned with your goals and strategy.

To set a take-profit, enter a market cap or price higher than your entry price. If you prefer to use a percentage, create an [Auto Order](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/settings/presets/spot-presets-auto-orders)
 instead.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/limit-orders/limit-sell#stop-loss)

Stop Loss


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set multiple Stop Loss, create separate orders with different market caps/prices and percentages aligned with your goals and strategy.

To set a stop-loss, enter a market cap or price lower than your entry price. For percentage-based stops, use [Auto Orders](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/settings/presets/spot-presets-auto-orders)
.

# Social Tasks Limit | Bloom Solana

To ensure optimal performance and efficiency, we’ve implemented 5 different tiers. This limit is designed to prevent traders from overloading the system by running too many tasks without effectively executing trades.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/twitter/social-tasks-limit#tiers)

Tiers


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tier

Tasks Limit

Platform Fee Tresholds

Tier 1

0-100

None

Tier 2

101-500

At least 5 SOL

Tier 3

501-1000

At least 10 SOL

Tier 4

1001-2000

At least 50 SOL

Tier 5

2000+

At least 100 SOL

Copy

    To run up to 100 tasks, there is no fee requirement.
    To run more than 100 tasks, each trader must have generated at least 5 SOL in platform fees.
    To run more than 500 tasks, each trader must have generated at least 10 SOL in platform fees.
    To run more than 1000 tasks, each trader must have generated at least 50 SOL in platform fees.
    To run more than 2000 tasks, each trader must have generated at least 100 SOL in platform fees.

What happens when you reach the task limit?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/twitter/social-tasks-limit#what-happens-when-you-reach-the-task-limit)

_Error creating task: you’ve reached the 100 tasks limit. To create more tasks, please generate an additional 3 SOL in platform fees to reach the 5 SOL target._

[PreviousSocial Limit Orders](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/twitter/social-limit-orders)
[NextPositions](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/positions)

Last updated 1 month ago

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. 🟢: When enabled, Bloom will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Profit/Loss %

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

Fixed Mcap

Set the target market cap at which you’d like Bloom to sell.

Mcap Variation

Set the market cap increase or decrease threshold at which you’d like Bloom to sell. Bloom will execute the sale only when the market cap change matches your specified value.

Sell at

This button adapts based on your selected selling method (Profit/Loss %, Fixed MCap, MCap Variation), allowing you to set your preferred value accordingly.

Enter your target value:

• Take Profit: e.g. 50%, 150%.

• Stop Loss: e.g. -20%, -50%.

Examples:

• Profit %: 100%: your holdings will be sold at 2x.

• Loss %: -50%: your holdings will be sold when the price drops by 50%.

Notes:

• Only one % value (TP or SL) per limit order.

Please enter your desired sell amount:

• For a sell of 10%, enter 10

Please enter your desired slippage:

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

High Impact (Expert only)

# Sniper Limit Orders | Bloom Solana

Sniper orders must be created upfront directly from `Settings->Presets->Sniper Presets`.

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

After creation, the task will automatically start post-buy. Make sure to delete it if you don't want it to run.

* * *

Click `📈 Spot Presets`.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FizbOeqyjo7rU4s9jnlNw%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252018.36.22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0c6e0b8-c99e-4737-b123-817f2c6bab02&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3efcc812&sv=2)

*   Click `📈 Limit Orders`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fpbi7IXYpA3u0jPckFhMz%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.32.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8716f39-a533-43f2-ba7d-439eec3becc2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9bb8dc78&sv=2)

*   Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIOnv8S50bInsqZrZbcI9%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.33.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a877771-6084-4509-9218-b2aecdbcd453&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc9df95f&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fq9yMAaFWzwPcoA3r3TsT%252FScreenshot%25202025-07-07%2520alle%252017.42.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ddc0678-a44d-48c1-bb69-44b189e9e853&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dff0b8cf&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. 🟢: When enabled, Bloom will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Profit/Loss %

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

Fixed Mcap

Set the target market cap at which you’d like Bloom to sell.

Mcap Variation

Set the market cap increase or decrease threshold at which you’d like Bloom to sell. Bloom will execute the sale only when the market cap change matches your specified value.

Sell at

This button adapts based on your selected selling method (Profit/Loss %, Fixed MCap, MCap Variation), allowing you to set your preferred value accordingly.

Enter your target value:

• Take Profit: e.g. 50%, 150%.

• Stop Loss: e.g. -20%, -50%.

Examples:

• Profit %: 100%: your holdings will be sold at 2x.

• Loss %: -50%: your holdings will be sold when the price drops by 50%.

Notes:

• Only one % value (TP or SL) per limit order.

Sell Amount

Set the target amount to sell as a percentage.

Please enter your desired sell amount:

Example:

• For a sell of 10%, enter 10

Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

High Impact (Expert only)

Enables trades that require higher price impact than usual. Use this if you’re buying large amounts of SOL in low-liquidity pools. ⚠️ **Expert users only:** using this when it’s not needed can route the sale through suboptimal pools or cause bad slippage.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fc3BThte0PlgtZal4UqJj%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252019.04.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1df5a62-a21c-414b-bb1f-d4800b8b224b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e02e17e&sv=2)

# Limit Buy | Bloom Solana

**Buy Fee –** The buy fee is taken from the default one in [settings](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/settings/fee)
.

**Orders expiration –** Expired orders are automatically deleted.

* * *

*   Start a regular [Buy](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/buy)
     task by entering the token address.
    
*   Tap `📈 Limit Orders`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F2wV7l4toZfy0NgzJscUK%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D760cfc85-22fa-4a40-95a8-72a0753c90bf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=306d97a8&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FipOAo8nUknvtNJWt9G84%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c0addbf-0058-4bf0-b2f0-042295050840&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=45a25205&sv=2)

Action

Response

Expiry

Set the order expiration time in hours (eg. 6).

Buy Amount

Choose the SOL amount to buy.

Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Buy Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

High Impact (Expert only)

Enables trades that require higher price impact than usual. Use this if you’re buying large amounts of SOL in low-liquidity pools.

⚠️ _**Expert users only:**_ _using this on tokens where it’s not needed may route your order through the wrong pool or lead to bad fills._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically buy the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. If enabled, the bot will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Market Cap

• Choose to create the order based on market cap. • Enter the target market cap value.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Price

• Choose to create the order based on price. • Enter the percentage of the current price at which you want to create the order.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Create Limit Order

# Withdraw | Bloom Solana

**Always keep your address locked when not making updates. It’s one of the most effective measures to protect your funds from unauthorized access or malicious attacks.**

* * *

*   Access `💸 Withdraw` easily from the home menu or by using the `/withdraw` command.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FoyeWAKuRNaLUIHMLIgaV%252FWithd.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7ec9c2b-e9bf-49cc-8ea9-801cddfb5504&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=16823df6&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F4kSVWmF4zzbP17j6B0sP%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb12963b-e466-47aa-ab0e-6c329cbb3059&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97fc42d6&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

50%, 100%

Preset percentage of SOL you want to withdraw (e.g., 50% withdraws half your funds).

X SOL

Edit the amount of SOL you wish to withdraw.

Set Address

Set the address to receive your funds.

Please enter your Solana withdrawal address:

Lock Address

Lock your address to prevent changes. This safety measure ensures that no malicious party can modify the address or withdraw your funds for 24 hours unlocking it.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FCtrv66BadLitK5Um2yYf%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252016.27.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f6d77d2-d63a-4974-98f1-14d5c9223d97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f911a15d&sv=2)

Unlock Address

Unlock your address if you need to make changes. A 24-hour security cooldown will be applied before any modifications are allowed.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F7lbgQtUAmgbWAke2uk7Q%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252016.27.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3700a0b-bb19-4746-8c87-4b3d734f8d6a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=78b93447&sv=2)

Back

Return to the previous page.

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/withdraw#locking-unlocking-withdraw-address)

Locking/Unlocking Withdraw Address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Protecting your funds is our top priority, and we’ve implemented a safety feature to help safeguard your wallet: Address Locking.

🔒 Why locking your address?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/withdraw#why-locking-your-address)

Locking your address ensures it cannot be changed while locked, making it impossible for anyone—including potential attackers—to replace it and withdraw your funds. This is a critical layer of security, especially in case of a malicious attack or if your wallet becomes compromised.

🔓 Unlocking your address[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/withdraw#unlocking-your-address)

If you need to make changes to your address, you must first unlock it. Once unlocked, a 24-hour security cooldown begins, ensuring that no changes can be made during this time. This delay provides a buffer to detect and prevent unauthorized attempts.

[PreviousPositions](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/positions)
[NextReferrals](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/referrals)

Last updated 5 days ago

Custom Sell


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Adjust the amount you want to sell by tapping `✏️ Sell Position`.

# Quick Query Ticker | Bloom Solana

The Quick Query Ticker feature lets you instantly retrieve essential token information directly through our Telegram bot. Simply input the token ticker using the `$` symbol followed by the ticker name (e.g., `$TRUMP`).

#### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/telegram-commands/quick-query-ticker#how-it-works)

How It Works:

1.  Open the Bloom Telegram bot.
    
2.  Type the ticker preceded by `$` (e.g., `$TICKER`).
    
3.  Hit send to instantly view the data.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FM8wiPpFDlJwlCHZBUStw%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520alle%252001.38.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd4a0e4d-e066-4728-bbbe-a0af28aaaa6b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=317ec0f9&sv=2)

# FAQs | Bloom Solana

Is Bloom Bot free to use?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#is-bloom-bot-free-to-use)

Yes, Bloom Bot is completely free to use. We only charge a 1% fee on buy and sell transactions.

What is slippage?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-slippage)

Slippage is the difference between the expected price of a trade and the actual price at which the trade is executed. It typically occurs during periods of high volatility or low liquidity. Generally, the higher it is, the faster your transaction is but the higher are the chances of getting your transaction sandwiched.

What is market cap?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-market-cap)

Market cap is the total value of a cryptocurrency, calculated by multiplying price by circulating supply.

What is a buy and sell fee?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-a-buy-and-sell-fee)

The fee you are willing to pay to get your transaction processed.

Buy & Sell Protection ON/OFF[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#buy-and-sell-protection-on-off)

🟩 **Buy/Sell Protection ON:**

Only MEV-protected processors are used, significantly reducing sandwich attack risk (though a minimal chance remains).

🟥 **Buy/Sell Protection OFF:**

Transactions are broadcasted to all supported processors, including those without MEV protection.

What is a bundle fee?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-a-bundle-fee)

A bundle tip fee is an extra payment made to JITO's network of block producers to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

When is the contract renounced?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#when-is-the-contract-renounced)

A contract is renounced when the developer gives up control, making it immutable and decentralized.

What is freeze authority?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-freeze-authority)

Freeze authority allows a contract owner to pause or restrict transfers of tokens, usually for security reasons.

What is liquidity?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-liquidity)

Liquidity in cryptocurrency markets refers to the total amount of funds available in the liquidity pool.

What is a liquidity pool?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-a-liquidity-pool)

A liquidity pool is a smart contract where tokens are locked for the purpose of providing liquidity.

How do Auto Orders work?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#how-do-auto-orders-work)

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

What does Degen Mode do?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-does-degen-mode-do)

Degen Mode instantly buys a token as soon as its contract address is entered in Telegram, without asking for additional details. Once typed, it will attempt to purchase based on your settings, regardless of your balance.

What are Limit Orders?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-are-limit-orders)

Limit Orders let you define a specific price at which you want to buy or sell a cryptocurrency. Unlike market orders that execute immediately at the current price, limit orders only trigger when the market reaches your desired price or market cap.

Bloom goes a step further by allowing you to combine multiple parameters—enabling you to fully customize each limit order to match your personal strategy.

What is a deployer?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-a-deployer)

A deployer is the wallet address that initially creates and launches a cryptocurrency contract on the blockchain.

The deployer field is an optional filter you can use to better manage your sniper tasks. Here, you can enter the deployer wallet address to make sure you’re sniping the correct token. You can skip this filter if you’ve already selected the right platform from the Platforms menu.

[PreviousChrome Extension](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/chrome-extension)
[NextSupported DEXes/Tokens](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/supported-dexes-tokens)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Sell | Bloom Solana

Spot sell provides all the tools and settings you need to sell a coin with one or multiple wallets, set limit orders, take profit, stop loss and perform any sell action according to your preferences.

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/sell#how-to-sell)

Multi-Wallet Sell


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To sell on multiple wallets, you need to select them first. Follow these steps:

*   Click `💰 Active Wallets`.
    
*   Activate or deactivate wallets based on your preferences.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FjM4uHCmk8RbqhRfnt1Zc%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252015.30.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3233dd19-d6d5-4a52-a688-adc38b31b5c0&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=16144c80&sv=2)

*   Once done, click `⬅️ Back` to return to the sell menu.

# Afk | Bloom Solana

AFK Mode allows you to automate your trades while you’re away. By setting up key parameters and configurations, the bot will automatically execute buy and sell orders on your behalf based on your inputs.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/afk#benefits-of-afk-mode)

**Benefits of AFK Mode**

1.  **Trade effortlessly**: You can potentially make profits even while you’re away, as the bot manages trades for you.
    
2.  **Tailored settings**: You control how the bot operates with various parameters, ensuring it aligns with your trading strategy.
    
3.  **Multi-Testing:** With AFK Mode, you can run multiple trading setups simultaneously to find the most profitable and reliable strategy.
    

Setting up AFK Mode properly requires time and effort. A well-configured setup can maximize your chances of success, but it’s essential to carefully adjust the parameters to fit your goals.

* * *

*   Access `💤 AFK Mode` easily from the home menu or by using the `/afk` command.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F4J9zRS4SI0MVIJoWShA8%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2dbb442-8c61-419f-af49-f2862b92c2e3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f76a89c&sv=2)

*   Tap `🆕 Add new config`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F2KVOsFXAiFEQecqFOSn9%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-04%2520alle%252015.48.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db584127d-c51b-4ce0-ace8-f140ac185a7c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d251d96a&sv=2)

# Bridge | Bloom Solana

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/bridge#what-bridging-means)

What bridging means?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bridging lets you move tokens from one blockchain (like Solana) to another (like Ethereum or Base) by locking or burning them on the original chain, then minting or unlocking an equivalent amount on the target chain. This process relies on cross-chain communication protocols or specialized smart contracts to verify that tokens were locked on the source chain before creating the new tokens on the destination. As a result, you maintain the same overall value while gaining access to DeFi opportunities that are unique to each blockchain.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/bridge#debridgepoints)

deBridgePoints

When you bridge through Bloom, you’ll earn deBridge points just as if you were bridging directly via deBridge itself.

* * *

*   Access `✈️ Bridge` easily from the home menu or by using the `/bridge` command.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FaGhMk0L8FdCwIRPu5btO%252Fsol.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfdb0b133-451f-4d32-8590-118f867701c1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=37e786df&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F5UgAzANOwwYnoiAHRh1V%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-30%2520alle%252017.09.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D071e23f3-acd5-4c26-bbd2-68512bd64de5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ccac3fd0&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/bridge#how-to-bridge)

How To Bridge


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From the SOL blockchain, you can directly bridge to BSC, Ethereum, and Base using Bloom.

*   SOL → BSC: Send SOL and receive BNB on BSC.
    
*   SOL → ETH: Send SOL and receive ETH on Ethereum.
    
*   SOL → BASE: Send SOL and receive ETH on Base.
    
*   SOL → HYPER EVM: Send SOL and receive HYPE on HYPER EVM.
    

*   Select the target receiver blockchain (BSC, ETH, BASE or HYPER EVM). Only one option can be active at a time.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FsPPZeBF171H0gaww58yt%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-30%2520alle%252017.09.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1fc73e27-c7ac-4301-b361-08eb4ff8be77&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=614ce07d&sv=2)

*   You can set the receiving addresses needed—(BSC, ETH, BASE, HYPER EVM)—depending on your needs. Tap `💸 Set Address`, then enter your receiver address for the blockchain you’ve selected.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FETtKkCjwstkY9vpDtQfX%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252013.48.14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D636e0733-b65a-4dd9-a905-fb7f86747e16&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cf668f5&sv=2)

*   Double-check that all details match, then tap `✈️ Bridge` to transfer your funds.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FNffEtgyfwvsTg9WOwdkB%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-10%2520alle%252015.52.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1cba66c3-2259-43d7-bc36-87752ac6baf1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4a1fd29&sv=2)

After bridging, if you’d like to switch the target receiving blockchain, ensure you select the new blockchain and eventually update the receiving wallet accordingly.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/bridge#locking-unlocking-withdraw-address)

Locking/Unlocking Withdraw Address


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Protecting your funds is our top priority, and we’ve implemented a safety feature to help safeguard your wallet: Address Locking.

Each address can be locked or unlocked independently.

Why locking your receiver address?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/bridge#why-locking-your-receiver-address)

Locking your receiver address ensures it cannot be changed while locked, making it impossible for anyone—including potential attackers—to replace it and bridge your funds. This is a critical layer of security, especially in case of a malicious attack or if your wallet becomes compromised.

Unlocking your receiver address[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/bridge#unlocking-your-receiver-address)

If you need to replace your receiver address, you must first unlock it. Once unlocked, a 24-hour security cooldown begins, ensuring that no changes can be made during this time. This delay provides a buffer to detect and prevent unauthorized attempts.

[PreviousReferrals](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/referrals)
[NextChrome Extension](https://solana.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/chrome-extension)

Last updated 5 days ago

# Copy | Bloom Solana

Copy-Trading allows you to mirror a target trader’s wallet by entering their address. Each copy-trading task can be fully customized through our settings to suit your specific needs.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/copy#before-you-start)

Before you start

✅ Ensure you set a [Copy-Trading Default Wallet](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/wallets)
.

🕒 Please wait 30 seconds after each change for it to take effect.

📝 **Changing your default wallet?** Remember to remake your tasks to use the new wallet for future transactions.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/copy#tipping-suggestios)

Tipping Suggestios

The higher the Bundle Tip (JITO), the lower the slippage should be. Conversely, the lower the Bundle Tip (JITO), the higher the slippage should be.

Without a JITO tip, the risk of getting MEV increases significantly.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot/copy#blacklist-info)

Blacklist Info

Adding an address to the blacklist applies across all your copy-trading configurations. This prevents any trades involving those addresses, regardless of the target wallet.

* * *

*   Access `🤖 Copy Trade` easily from the home menu or by using the `/copy` command.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FzRjPGca4qXTXiXAFZ6ZD%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D735f0953-f1a1-4ee6-b682-6334a558f296&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cd22edf7&sv=2)

*   Tap `🆕 Add new config`.

Email Protection
================

You are unable to access this email address bloombot.app
--------------------------------------------------------

.

1.  Choose the SOL amount to sell.

`Please enter your desired amount: (SOL, %, hours)`

Set the order expiration time in hours (eg. 6H).

`Please enter your desired amount: (SOL, %, hours)`

Bundle Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount: (SOL, %, hours)`

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount: (SOL, %, hours)`

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. If enabled, the bot will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🔴: Inactive

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-sell#take-profit)

Take Profit


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set multiple Take Profits, create separate orders with different market caps/prices and percentages aligned with your goals and strategy.

Follow the steps below to set up your take profit strategy.

1.  Enter the Take Profit percentage with `+` in front of the value (eg. +50) in `💰 Market Cap` or `💰 Price` according to your target.
    
2.  Setup the order as a regular Limit Sell one.
    

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-sell#stop-loss)

Stop Loss


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Follow the steps below to set up your stop loss strategy.

1.  Enter the Stop Loss percentage with `-` in front of the value (eg. -50) in `💰 Market Cap` or `💰 Price` according to your target.
    
2.  Setup the order as a regular Limit Sell one.
    

Last updated 3 months ago

# Limit Orders | Bloom Solana

Limit orders allow you to set a specific price at which you want to buy or sell a cryptocurrency. Unlike market orders that execute immediately at the current price, limit orders only trigger when the market reaches your desired price or market cap.

Additionally, you can customize your order with multiple parameters, ensuring your trade is tailored to your strategy.

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-buy)

![Cover](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIHItN0YmARiqkuJlrEYR%252FBloom_Background_2K.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D546957d6-ed07-409e-96ff-bf8839b684c3&width=245&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fab55910&sv=2)

# Buy | Bloom Solana

Spot Buy provides all the tools and settings you need to purchase a coin with one or multiple wallets, set limit orders, and perform any buy action according to your preferences.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/buy#how-to-buy)

How to Buy


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter the target token address (eg. `Z6TpfVZySS4vWcHrF22yzsa7nZRXQBKu2qjF9bNpump`) or click `↔️ Switch to Buy` from the sell menu.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FLxLdPPlXNAkqrYilqUTb%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252015.29.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc778f0c6-4bc2-4f5a-b820-61e2cbf237a9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5050b2e&sv=2)

Action

Response

# Sell | Bloom Solana

Spot sell provides all the tools and settings you need to sell a coin with one or multiple wallets, set limit orders, take profit, stop loss and perform any sell action according to your preferences.

* * *

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FVjuRY0iP9MjKS7y0SdhV%252FScreenshot%25202024-12-13%2520alle%252015.45.55.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52bd5630-a6c8-496d-84dc-9f82415462c1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=32fc99b5&sv=2)

How to Sell


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

2.  Set the slippage percentage.
    
3.  Select the percentage you’d like to sell. Choose a preset or enter a custom value.

# Sniper Presets | Bloom Solana

Sniper Presets allow you to set the default configurations used when sniping a coin.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/settings/presets/sniper-presets#mev-protect)

MEV Protect

*   `Normal Mode:` – MEV Protect is ON 🟢 by default.
    
*   `PRO Mode:` – MEV Protect is OFF 🔴 by default.

Max Fee

Set the maximum fee you’re willing to pay for a successful transaction. The fee charged will range between your Min Fee and Max Fee amounts.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIGqDYxeSfo3B3Z5BcBRh%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-18%2520alle%252015.25.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54c17f5a-a20d-440f-b2cc-0fb3b931bcac&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db4697d3&sv=2)

Min Fee

Set the minimum fee amount you’d be charged if the transaction fails. You won’t be charged more than this value in case of failure.

`Please enter the minimum amount out. You can enter a number with K/M suffixes or enter -1 to disable:`

# Copy | Bloom Solana

Copy-Trading allows you to mirror a target trader’s wallet by entering their address. Each copy-trading task can be fully customized through our settings to suit your specific needs.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy#before-you-start)

Before you start

✅ Ensure you set a [Copy-Trading Default Wallet](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/wallets#wallet-settings)
.

🕒 Please wait 30 seconds after each change for it to take effect.

📝 **Changing your default wallet?** Remember to remake your tasks to use the new wallet for future transactions.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy#tipping-suggestios)

Tipping Suggestios

The higher the Bundle Tip (JITO), the lower the slippage should be. Conversely, the lower the Bundle Tip (JITO), the higher the slippage should be.

Without a JITO tip, the risk of getting MEV increases significantly.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy#blacklist-info)

Blacklist Info

Adding an address to the blacklist applies across all your copy-trading configurations. This prevents any trades involving those addresses, regardless of the target wallet.

* * *

Access the copy-tading menu directly by using the `/copy` command or from the `/start` menu.

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy#setup)

Setup


------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F7RwXfcpaJOdgui19lwT1%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-10%2520alle%252018.05.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1caa6c68-5f37-48ae-86fb-1b3873808991&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bdad4871&sv=2)

🔴 – The copy-trading profile is **inactive**.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FISdSLjP4kIVvpgesP2iv%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-10%2520alle%252018.05.35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54347e2a-53e4-4070-95dd-9f2ee68c4226&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=92fb8cd1&sv=2)

# Slippage | Bloom Solana

Slippage is the difference between the expected price of a trade and the actual price at which the trade is executed. It typically occurs during periods of high volatility or low liquidity. Generally, the higher it is, the faster your transaction is but the higher are the chances of getting your transaction sandwiched.

* * *

1.  Run `/orders` command.
    
2.  You will be prompted to the following menu, where you can view the coins with active orders. ![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FjJ47SUfsdzz6P989c8My%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-16%2520alle%252013.29.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a778e9f-ca6e-46ad-a050-0c3bf01c0802&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2860ae9f&sv=2)

The menu shown in the image below will appear. ![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FtPeKLASast9rgXSGG14x%252Flo1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fc83ca1-8dec-4408-baff-7f22226732ef&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4995c42&sv=2)
    
4.  This menu provides an overview of all your current open orders for the selected coin. By clicking `🗑️ Delete Order`, you can cancel the corresponding order displayed on the left. _eg._ ![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FXhEroZEPFFmNt9FNBjDe%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-16%2520alle%252013.41.01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5283f7a9-f460-46f9-88bc-4afadf9670ea&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6640ebea&sv=2) _By clicking_ `_🗑️ Delete Order_`_, you will delete the_ `_🤑 Limit Buy (#1)_` _order._

# Degen Mode | Bloom Solana

Degen Mode instantly buys a token as soon as its contract address is entered in Telegram, without asking for additional details. Once typed, it will attempt to purchase based on your settings, regardless of your balance.

*   When enabled, Degen Mode will attempt to **buy immediately as soon as the token address is entered**, even before the token menu appears. It will try to execute the purchase regardless of the wallet balance.
    
*   Once the token is sold, it won’t attempt to rebuy, even if auto-buy is enabled.
    

**🟢 ON –** Automatically buy a coin when the coin address is pasted. 🔴 **OFF –** Manually start buy when the coin address is pasted.

* * *

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F0Ky6DnyX74lGE0RdXmu7%252FScreenshot%25202024-12-25%2520alle%252018.29.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3df4a5f-2c12-4196-bd6b-4068d1e09b8b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d292ad1&sv=2)

*   Click `🟢🔴 Degen Mode`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FmCeJFC4KkfiPW2NppTiM%252FScreenshot%25202024-12-16%2520alle%252000.00.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b13b50d-3f5d-4da2-9e99-f9608e9af965&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=49bb0d15&sv=2)

# Withdraw | Bloom Solana

**Always keep your address locked when not making updates. It’s one of the most effective measures to protect your funds from unauthorized access or malicious attacks.**

* * *

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F2CP550QaahzN07i7LFlU%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3be49d83-5845-4926-8fc9-1b80f88f8a1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4329982a&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

50%, 100%

Preset percentage of SOL you want to withdraw (e.g., 50% withdraws half your funds).

X SOL

Edit the amount of SOL you wish to withdraw.

Set Address

Set the address to receive your funds.

`Please enter your Solana withdrawal address:`

Lock Address

Lock your address to prevent changes. This safety measure ensures that no malicious party can modify the address or withdraw your funds for 24 hours unlocking it.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FbPZJXWwAcfj7g1Bhy4q0%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-18%2520alle%252021.18.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda901c40-5b33-4045-bbe6-1c6b4576e30f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8de0fff6&sv=2)

Unlock Address

Unlock your address if you need to make changes. A 24-hour security cooldown will be applied before any modifications are allowed.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FJJzR01mYXeGTBoJWOrh9%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-18%2520alle%252021.09.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46fb1a56-557c-4e23-99e1-afa07d902530&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f560530&sv=2)

Back

Return to the previous page.

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/withdraw#locking-unlocking-withdraw-address)

Locking/Unlocking Withdraw Address


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Protecting your funds is our top priority, and we’ve implemented a safety feature to help safeguard your wallet: Address Locking.

🔒 Why locking your address?[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/withdraw#why-locking-your-address)

Locking your address ensures it cannot be changed while locked, making it impossible for anyone—including potential attackers—to replace it and withdraw your funds. This is a critical layer of security, especially in case of a malicious attack or if your wallet becomes compromised.

🔓 Unlocking your address[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/withdraw#unlocking-your-address)

If you need to make changes to your address, you must first unlock it. Once unlocked, a 24-hour security cooldown begins, ensuring that no changes can be made during this time. This delay provides a buffer to detect and prevent unauthorized attempts.

Last updated 2 months ago

---
