# Afk | Bloom Solana

AFK Mode allows you to automate your trades while you’re away. By setting up key parameters and configurations, the bot will automatically execute buy and sell orders on your behalf based on your inputs.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/afk#benefits-of-afk-mode)

**Benefits of AFK Mode**

1.  **Trade effortlessly**: You can potentially make profits even while you’re away, as the bot manages trades for you.
    
2.  **Tailored settings**: You control how the bot operates with various parameters, ensuring it aligns with your trading strategy.
    
3.  **Multi-Testing:** With AFK Mode, you can run multiple trading setups simultaneously to find the most profitable and reliable strategy.
    

Setting up AFK Mode properly requires time and effort. A well-configured setup can maximize your chances of success, but it’s essential to carefully adjust the parameters to fit your goals.

* * *

Access `💤 AFK Mode` easily from the home menu or by using the `/afk` command.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FmqFxGqVFNhf7JrndECEO%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bae0acf-462a-440d-99ef-07ec27f13051&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c3b6a37b&sv=2)

*   Tap `🆕 Add new config`.

# Normal Mode | Bloom Solana

Sniping is crucial for fast trades during Pumpfun migrations, Moonshot migrations, and Raydium new liquidity pools. It helps you send transactions quickly, outpacing the competition when timing is critical.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#before-you-start)

Before you start

Ensure you set a [Sniper Default Wallet](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/wallets#wallet-settings)
.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#id-3-pending-transactions)

3 Pending Transactions

Don’t be alarmed if you see three pending messages when you initiate a sniper task. The sniper sends one transaction from each of our servers, but only one of the three pending transactions will be confirmed.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#mev-protect)

MEV Protect

On Normal Mode **MEV Protect is enabled** by default.

### 

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#tipping-suggestios)

Tipping Suggestios

The higher the Buy or Sell Tip (Processors), the lower the slippage should be. Conversely, the lower the Buy or Sell Tip (Processors), the higher the slippage should be.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#interactive-tutorial)

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#sell-reverse-sniper)

Sell (Reverse Sniper)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Reverse sniping is used when you've already bought a coin un Pump.fun and want to sell it instantly when it migrates to Raydium. It works like sniping, but instead of buying, you’re selling.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FhjgwM5LNclwCP2oECR0E%252FScreenshot%25202025-01-09%2520alle%252017.41.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db73af4a2-9678-42d7-b029-0e5e50ad3e1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cd5fda7b&sv=2)

1.  To reverse snipe, either run the `/sniper` command or click `🎯 LP Sniper` in the main menu.
    
2.  Tap `🎯 Create Task` or click on an already existing one.
    
3.  Click `🔄 Switch to Sell`.
    
4.  Set it up
    

Button

Action

Action

Switch to Buy

[Refer to the dedicated guide.](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana-bot/sniper#create-sniper-task)

Sell Amount

Choose the % to sell.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FsWCkhqsHP7X4epT0Mdu6%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-18%2520alle%252015.25.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88d4126d-f6fb-408a-9a33-5c292e2716e0&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ce61abb&sv=2)

Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIGqDYxeSfo3B3Z5BcBRh%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-18%2520alle%252015.25.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54c17f5a-a20d-440f-b2cc-0fb3b931bcac&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db4697d3&sv=2)

# Spot Presets • Auto Orders | Bloom Solana

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

After creation, the task will automatically start post-buy. Make sure to delete it if you don't want it to run.

* * *

*   Click `📈 Spot Presets`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FxPo0UWBnRvSLqudJqvVb%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252013.59.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8a463dcb-b5c2-47b3-b6e7-15a16d0e284a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2a3b504f&sv=2)

*   Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fo2s6fTl90yXDHGPFJ15A%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-06%2520alle%252018.48.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D148b32d1-d95f-48a7-bade-5c61b0f44e97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57326ed6&sv=2)

# PRO Mode | Bloom Solana

PRO Mode is a custom-developed feature designed to significantly enhance sniping performance. While we can’t disclose all the details, here’s what you need to know:

1.  The **fastest processor** is automatically use to maximize the success of your snipe.
    
2.  **Successful Transactions:** You’ll never spend more than your Max Fee.
    
3.  **Failed Transactions:** The amount you pay won’t exceed your Min Fee amount.
    
4.  It’s recommended to set your Max Priority Fee lower than your Max Total Fee for optimal cost management.
    
5.  No MEV Protection – If you require MEV protection, switch to Normal Mode.
    
6.  To create a PRO account, your wallet **must have balance**. Wallets with zero balance cannot be upgraded to PRO.
    

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/pro-mode#interactive-tutorial)

Interactive Tutorial


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

1.  To access the sniper menu, either run the `/sniper` command or click `🎯 LP Sniper` in the main menu.
    
    ![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FclcHDUomJViTd4QS9Wcu%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D079453e6-29ca-42e5-a60d-c6fc790208d4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=493c2caf&sv=2)
    
2.  Access the pro account menu by clicking `🎯 Pro Accounts`.
    
3.  Turn a sniper account PRO by clicking `⚡️ Create PRO`.
    
    ![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FCFyUoI9DTcQMCDvLzE8K%252Fpro%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e45c765-e4b2-4d65-b499-5c7eca69053f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf52c688&sv=2)
    
4.  Update the status by clicking `🔄 Refresh`.

Sell (Reverse Sniper)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Reverse sniping is used when you've already bought a coin un Pump.fun and want to sell it instantly when it migrates to Raydium. It works like sniping, but instead of buying, you’re selling.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fz8b6eXAnxXFMfxx3KPdA%252FScreenshot%25202025-01-09%2520alle%252017.43.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5f9b680-3c35-4064-b51f-3d01685bb2cc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14103967&sv=2)

1.  To reverse snipe, either run the `/sniper` command or click `🎯 LP Sniper` in the main menu.
    
2.  Tap `🎯 Create Task` or click on an already existing one.
    
3.  Click `🔄 Switch to Sell`.
    
4.  Set it up

# Copy Presets | Bloom Solana

Copy Presets allow you to set the default configurations used when running a copy-trading task.

* * *

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FoLbpAqeJGEJuYd42YMan%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252013.59.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc333c3ac-a552-4769-be91-892cd927f355&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c13e1ea7&sv=2)

*   Click `🤖 Copy Presets`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FB4tydxmadqFycCgxwPpj%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-10%2520alle%252018.07.15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57d26e4b-dbc1-49fd-8980-ac4b9b7aee4a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=baa5baef&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Max Traded Token

Set the maximum number of coins the bot will purchase according to your current configuration.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

First Interaction

🟢: If enabled, it will trigger trades only when the trader you’re copy-trading interacts with the token for the first time 🔴: If disabled, the bot will not consider whether the trader has previously interacted with the token or not.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Max Buy

Set the maximum amount you’re willing to buy, regardless of the amount purchased by the target wallet. _**Max Buy applies to each transaction.**_

`Please enter your desired max buy amount in SOL:`

Buy Exact

Buy the same SOL amount as the target wallet.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy %

Buy a percentage of the amount the target wallet buys. _You can set it above 100% to purchase more than the target wallet (eg. 130% buys an additional 30% of the amount purchased by the target wallet)._

`Buy Amount: Set it to the desired percentage to turn it on`

Buy Fixed

Buy a fixed SOL amount, regardless of the target wallet’s amount.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Min MCap

Set the minimum market cap you are willing to buy at.

`Please enter your desired market cap (eg: 12M / 1K / 10000):`

Max MCap

Set the maximum market cap you are willing to buy at.

`Please enter your desired market cap (eg: 12M / 1K / 10000):`

Follow Sell

Choose whether to sell when the target wallet sells.

_When enabled, the bot will mirror the selling percentage of the trader - for example, if they sell 50% of their position, the bot will also sell 50% of your position_

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Only Once

Buy the coin only once, even if the target wallet makes multiple purchases. _If you’re using multiple wallets, ensure it’s turned ON for each one._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Sell Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Buy Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Sell Slippage

Set the sell slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Mev Protect

The fastest processor is automatically used to ensure maximum transaction success, whether MEV Protection is ON or OFF.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Sell Tip

Set the target sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Limit Orders

[Refer to the dedicated guide.](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy/copy-limit-orders)

⬅️Back

Return to the previous page.

• 📉 Stop Loss: _Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)_

`Please enter your desired amount:`

`Please enter your desired amount:`

`Please enter your desired amount:`

# Afk Presets | Bloom Solana

AFK Presets allow you to set the default configurations used when running an AFK Mode task.

* * *

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fsm85EhUSlMNkGF7qyHxG%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252013.59.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc21a1c6-cf85-4b31-a13e-1ce9a824e610&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=45456fac&sv=2)

*   Click `💤 AFK Presets`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FKpYYE0gJ7wpjz5oMTlW2%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252014.00.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ab71f48-ed8a-4e94-86e4-3d54b1357efb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9bb9b8f1&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Max Traded Token

Set the maximum number of coins the bot will purchase according to your current configuration.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Buy

Choose the SOL amount to buy.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Mev Protect

The fastest processor is automatically used to ensure maximum transaction success, whether MEV Protection is ON or OFF.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Twitter Tweet

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys tweeted contracts according to your settings. _(Including quoted retweets where the contract is taken from the quoted text)._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Twitter Reply

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in a Tweet reply according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Twitter Bio Update

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in bio the moment the bio changes according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Twitter Retweet

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in the original retweeted post, following your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Pre Bonding PF

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys PumpFun contracts according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Other/After Bonding

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys non-PumpFun tokens (e.g., Orca, Raydium) according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Min Market Cap

Set the minimum market cap you are willing to buy at.

`Please enter your desired market cap (eg: 12M / 1K / 10000):`

Max Market Cap

Set the maximum market cap you are willing to buy at.

`Please enter your desired market cap (eg: 12M / 1K / 10000):`

Min Token Age

• Set the minimum amount of time passed since the token was created. • For Pump.fun migrated coins, the time is calculated from the moment they bonded.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Ft9BHc1dP9dZQtQcFKeff%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252014.07.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54590192-0325-458f-8de6-440387995fda&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f6cff3b&sv=2)

Max Token Age

• Set the maximum amount of time passed since the token was created. • For Pump.fun migrated coins, the time is calculated from the moment they bonded.

* * *

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/settings/presets/afk-presets#auto-orders)

Auto Orders


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

After creation, the task will automatically start post-buy. Make sure to delete it if you don't want it to run.

*   Click `📈 Limit Orders`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FK1Fv1gnxZtsr59A273xA%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252014.27.37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd079dab5-fb57-448e-a4e8-815e282b8e15&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66030db5&sv=2)

*   Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`.
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fo2s6fTl90yXDHGPFJ15A%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-06%2520alle%252018.48.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D148b32d1-d95f-48a7-bade-5c61b0f44e97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57326ed6&sv=2)

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FiJ2yM7FjOg5bCfjU1ShW%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-06%2520alle%252018.46.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D840abc62-e00a-4303-9aaf-1879b8af1551&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9fa5accf&sv=2)

Dev Sell

🟢: Active

• 📉 Stop Loss: _Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)_

# Afk Limit Orders | Bloom Solana

[](https://solana.bloombot.app/solana-bot-1.0-old/afk/afk-limit-orders#interactive-tutorial)

Interactive Tutorial


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

1.  Click on `💤 AFK Mode` in the home menu or use the `/afk` command.
    
2.  Click `🆕 Add New Config` or and already existing config.
    
3.  Click `📈 Limit Orders`.
    
    ![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fd8koh7Wwb3JKX9j2SVZE%252Flo%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc984936-a35f-426f-a4a8-29e48f3bf64e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=952547a&sv=2)
    
4.  Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`. ![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FRVzoSYfI5lrM4Ys4agzZ%252Flm23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b9c180c-16a3-40fe-9b7a-c850ecb57be5&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3735a00d&sv=2)
    

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FSUZOyb1nJOYfkzWeufQX%252FScreenshot%25202024-12-17%2520alle%252019.44.15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D646d146b-650b-401f-b92a-ae879b304c81&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58940362&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Sell Amount

Enter the % to be sold for the Take Profit and Stop Loss.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Profit/Loss

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Bundle Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. If enabled 🟢, the bot will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

![](https://solana.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FPnYU0w7yMznKDOcEcmZd%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-31%2520alle%252017.54.56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87552933-0fcc-41b4-b618-ea8d93bef52e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b2e120f&sv=2)
